            Cells(m + 11, n + -1).FormulaR1C1 = "=R[-27]C"
            Cells(m + 11, n + 0).FormulaR1C1 = "0"
            Cells(m + 11, n + 1).FormulaR1C1 = "=R[-27]C"

            Cells(m + 3, n + 1).Font.name = "Calibri"

            Cells(m1 + 1, n1 + 1).Value = ""
       Call AddNewVector
      End If ' vector ends
      If m = m1 + 117 Then ' vector 1
            Cells(m + 3, n + -1).FormulaR1C1 = "=R[-9]C+1"

            Cells(m + 5, n + 1).FormulaR1C1 = "=R37C7"

            Cells(m + 7, n + 1).FormulaR1C1 = "=R[-7]C+R[-9]C"

            Cells(m + 8, n + 2).FormulaR1C1 = "=IF(R[-4]C[-1]>1,"" <-- Variable coordinates"","""")"

            Cells(m + 9, n + 0).FormulaR1C1 = "=(-R[-18]C[-1]*R[-9]C[1]+R[-18]C[1]*R[-9]C[-1])*R[-12]C"
            Cells(m + 9, n + 1).FormulaR1C1 = "=(R[-18]C[-2]*R[-9]C[-1]-R[-18]C[-1]*R[-9]C[-2])*R[-12]C[-1]"
            Cells(m + 9, n + 2).FormulaR1C1 = "=""B_""&R[-24]C[-1]"
            Cells(m + 10, n + -1).FormulaR1C1 = "=R[-27]C"
            Cells(m + 10, n + 0).FormulaR1C1 = "0"
            Cells(m + 10, n + 1).FormulaR1C1 = "=R[-27]C"
            Cells(m + 10, n + 4).FormulaR1C1 = "=IF(RC[-4]>0,""       For aditional formula (FA),"","""")"
            Cells(m + 11, n + -1).FormulaR1C1 = "=R[-27]C"

            Cells(m + 11, n + 4).FormulaR1C1 = "=IF(R[-1]C[-4]>0,""<--  use these cells."","""")"
            Cells(m + 3, n + 1).Interior.Color = "255"
            Cells(m + 3, n + 1).Font.Size = "11"
            Cells(m + 3, n + 1).Font.name = "Calibri"
            Cells(m + 4, n - 1).Value = 1
            Cells(m1 + 1, n1 + 1).Value = ""
       Cells(m1 + 2, n1 - 1).Value = 14
      End If ' vector ends
      If m = m1 + 117 Then
       Call BlackWhiteDesk
       Call PutEqBut
      End If ' actualizar hoja
